Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists of Grand Prix Bologna 2017
=============================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 6, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











The main event only started on Saturday morning, but the action already began on Friday. Naturally, we were most interested in the Last-Chance Trials run that day, as those results actually influenced the Grand Prix itself, by awarding byes to all winners. Plus, their decklists could provide a first idea of what to expect over the course of the weekend and beyond.







#### David Toth, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)





[Decklist](#none)
